I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Batch publish - support isolated reads
### Observed behavior

We currently don't support isolated reads for batch publish, meaning once you batch publish 10 messages any readers through message GET requests or consumers will observe these messages as they are applied sequentially and not as one atomic action. Due to that a reader could observe parts of the batch's effects, even if the full batch was committed.

Likely this is already an issue when using `Nats-Rollup`, since the rollup happens separately after persisting the message that contains the rollup. Which would mean you could observe the full stream including the rollup message in a read, even if the rollup should have purged data and not allowed you to see the previous messages within the same read.

### Expected behavior

Support isolated reads in the server, guaranteeing that readers are also "aware" of the batch semantics and either observe none of a batch's effects, or observe it in its entirety after commit.

### Server and client version

`main`

### Host environment

_No response_

### Steps to reproduce

_No response_

</pr_description>

    14	package server
    15	
    16	import (
    17	        "encoding/json"
    18	        "errors"
    19	        "fmt"
    20	        "math"
    21	        "math/big"
    22	        "path/filepath"
    23	        "slices"
    24	        "strings"
    25	        "sync"
    26	        "sync/atomic"
    27	        "time"
    28	)
    29	
    30	var (
    31	        // Tracks the total inflight batches, across all streams and accounts that enable batching.
    32	        globalInflightBatches atomic.Int32
    33	)
    34	
    35	type batching struct {
    36	        mu    sync.Mutex
    37	        group map[string]*batchGroup
    38	}
    39	
    40	type batchGroup struct {
    41	        lseq  uint64
    42	        store StreamStore
    43	        timer *time.Timer
    44	}
    45	
    46	// Lock should be held.
    47	func (batches *batching) newBatchGroup(mset *stream, batchId string) (*batchGroup, error) {
    48	        store, err := newBatchStore(mset, batchId)
    49	        if err != nil {
    50	                return nil, err
    51	        }
    52	        b := &batchGroup{store: store}
    53	
    54	        // Create a timer to clean up after timeout.
    55	        timeout := streamMaxBatchTimeout
    56	        if maxBatchTimeout := mset.srv.getOpts().JetStreamLimits.MaxBatchTimeout; maxBatchTimeout > 0 {
    57	                timeout = maxBatchTimeout
    58	        }
    59	        b.timer = time.AfterFunc(timeout, func() {
    60	                b.cleanup(batchId, batches)
    61	        })
    62	        return b, nil
    63	}
    64	
    65	func getBatchStoreDir(mset *stream, batchId string) (string, string) {
    66	        mset.mu.RLock()
    67	        jsa, name := mset.jsa, mset.cfg.Name
    68	        mset.mu.RUnlock()
    69	
    70	        jsa.mu.RLock()
    71	        sd := jsa.storeDir
    72	        jsa.mu.RUnlock()
    73	
    74	        bname := getHash(batchId)
    75	        return bname, filepath.Join(sd, streamsDir, name, batchesDir, bname)
    76	}
    77	
    78	func newBatchStore(mset *stream, batchId string) (StreamStore, error) {
    79	        mset.mu.RLock()
    80	        replicas, storage := mset.cfg.Replicas, mset.cfg.Storage
    81	        mset.mu.RUnlock()
    82	
    83	        if replicas == 1 && storage == FileStorage {
    84	                bname, storeDir := getBatchStoreDir(mset, batchId)
    85	                fcfg := FileStoreConfig{AsyncFlush: true, BlockSize: defaultLargeBlockSize, StoreDir: storeDir}
    86	                s := mset.srv
    87	                prf := s.jsKeyGen(s.getOpts().JetStreamKey, mset.acc.Name)
    88	                if prf != nil {
    89	                        // We are encrypted here, fill in correct cipher selection.
    90	                        fcfg.Cipher = s.getOpts().JetStreamCipher
    91	                }
    92	                oldprf := s.jsKeyGen(s.getOpts().JetStreamOldKey, mset.acc.Name)
    93	                cfg := StreamConfig{Name: bname, Storage: FileStorage}
    94	                return newFileStoreWithCreated(fcfg, cfg, time.Time{}, prf, oldprf)
    95	        }
    96	        return newMemStore(&StreamConfig{Name: _EMPTY_, Storage: MemoryStorage})
    97	}
    98	
    99	// readyForCommit indicates the batch is ready to be committed.
   100	// If the timer has already cleaned up the batch, we can't commit.
   101	// Otherwise, we ensure the timer does not clean up the batch in the meantime.
   102	// Lock should be held.
   103	func (b *batchGroup) readyForCommit() bool {
   104	        if !b.timer.Stop() {
   105	                return false
   106	        }
   107	        b.store.FlushAllPending()
   108	        return true
   109	}
   110	
   111	// cleanup deletes underlying resources associated with the batch and unregisters it from the stream's batches.
   112	func (b *batchGroup) cleanup(batchId string, batches *batching) {
   113	        batches.mu.Lock()
   114	        defer batches.mu.Unlock()
   115	        b.cleanupLocked(batchId, batches)
   116	}
   117	
   118	// Lock should be held.
   119	func (b *batchGroup) cleanupLocked(batchId string, batches *batching) {
   120	        globalInflightBatches.Add(-1)
   121	        b.timer.Stop()
   122	        b.store.Delete(true)
   123	        delete(batches.group, batchId)
   124	}
   125	
   126	// Lock should be held.
   127	func (b *batchGroup) stopLocked() {
   128	        globalInflightBatches.Add(-1)
   129	        b.timer.Stop()
   130	        b.store.Stop()
   131	}
   132	
   133	// batchStagedDiff stages all changes for consistency checks until commit.
   134	type batchStagedDiff struct {
   135	        msgIds             map[string]struct{}
   136	        counter            map[string]*msgCounterRunningTotal
   137	        inflight           map[string]*inflightSubjectRunningTotal
   138	        expectedPerSubject map[string]*batchExpectedPerSubject
   139	}
   140	
   141	type batchExpectedPerSubject struct {
   142	        sseq  uint64 // Stream sequence.
   143	        clseq uint64 // Clustered proposal sequence.
   144	}
   145	
   146	func (diff *batchStagedDiff) commit(mset *stream) {
   147	        if len(diff.msgIds) > 0 {
   148	                ts := time.Now().UnixNano()
   149	                mset.ddMu.Lock()
   150	                for msgId := range diff.msgIds {
   151	                        // We stage with zero, and will update in processJetStreamMsg once we know the sequence.
   152	                        mset.storeMsgIdLocked(&ddentry{msgId, 0, ts})
   153	                }
   154	                mset.ddMu.Unlock()
   155	        }
   156	
   157	        // Store running totals for counters, we could have multiple counter increments proposed, but not applied yet.
   158	        if len(diff.counter) > 0 {
   159	                if mset.clusteredCounterTotal == nil {
   160	                        mset.clusteredCounterTotal = make(map[string]*msgCounterRunningTotal, len(diff.counter))
   161	                }
   162	                for k, c := range diff.counter {
   163	                        mset.clusteredCounterTotal[k] = c
   164	                }
   165	        }
   166	
   167	        // Track inflight.
   168	        if len(diff.inflight) > 0 {
   169	                if mset.inflight == nil {
   170	                        mset.inflight = make(map[string]*inflightSubjectRunningTotal, len(diff.inflight))
   171	                }
   172	                for subj, i := range diff.inflight {
   173	                        if c, ok := mset.inflight[subj]; ok {
   174	                                c.bytes += i.bytes
   175	                                c.ops += i.ops
   176	                        } else {
   177	                                mset.inflight[subj] = i
   178	                        }
   179	                }
   180	        }
   181	
   182	        // Track sequence and subject.
   183	        if len(diff.expectedPerSubject) > 0 {
   184	                if mset.expectedPerSubjectSequence == nil {
   185	                        mset.expectedPerSubjectSequence = make(map[uint64]string, len(diff.expectedPerSubject))
   186	                }
   187	                if mset.expectedPerSubjectInProcess == nil {
   188	                        mset.expectedPerSubjectInProcess = make(map[string]struct{}, len(diff.expectedPerSubject))
   189	                }
   190	                for subj, e := range diff.expectedPerSubject {
   191	                        mset.expectedPerSubjectSequence[e.clseq] = subj
   192	                        mset.expectedPerSubjectInProcess[subj] = struct{}{}
   193	                }
   194	        }
   195	}
   196	
   197	type batchApply struct {
   198	        mu         sync.Mutex
   199	        id         string            // ID of the current batch.
   200	        count      uint64            // Number of entries in the batch, for consistency checks.
   201	        entries    []*CommittedEntry // Previous entries that are part of this batch.
   202	        entryStart int               // The index into an entry indicating the first message of the batch.
   203	        maxApplied uint64            // Applied value before the entry containing the first message of the batch.
   204	}
   205	
   206	// clearBatchStateLocked clears in-memory apply-batch-related state.
   207	// batch.mu lock should be held.
   208	func (batch *batchApply) clearBatchStateLocked() {
   209	        batch.id = _EMPTY_
   210	        batch.count = 0
   211	        batch.entries = nil
   212	        batch.entryStart = 0
   213	        batch.maxApplied = 0
   214	}
   215	
   216	// rejectBatchStateLocked rejects the batch and clears in-memory apply-batch-related state.
   217	// Corrects mset.clfs to take the failed batch into account.
   218	// batch.mu lock should be held.
   219	func (batch *batchApply) rejectBatchStateLocked(mset *stream) {
   220	        mset.clMu.Lock()
   221	        mset.clfs += batch.count
   222	        mset.clMu.Unlock()
   223	        // We're rejecting the batch, so all entries need to be returned to the pool.
   224	        for _, bce := range batch.entries {
   225	                bce.ReturnToPool()
   226	        }
   227	        batch.clearBatchStateLocked()
   228	}
   229	
   230	func (batch *batchApply) rejectBatchState(mset *stream) {
   231	        batch.mu.Lock()
   232	        defer batch.mu.Unlock()
   233	        batch.rejectBatchStateLocked(mset)
   234	}
   235	
   236	// checkMsgHeadersPreClusteredProposal checks the message for expected/consistency headers.
   237	// mset.mu lock must NOT be held or used.
   238	// mset.clMu lock must be held.
   239	func checkMsgHeadersPreClusteredProposal(
   240	        diff *batchStagedDiff, mset *stream, subject string, hdr []byte, msg []byte, sourced bool, name string,
   241	        jsa *jsAccount, allowRollup, denyPurge, allowTTL, allowMsgCounter, allowMsgSchedules bool,
   242	        discard DiscardPolicy, discardNewPer bool, maxMsgSize int, maxMsgs int64, maxMsgsPer int64, maxBytes int64,
   243	) ([]byte, []byte, uint64, *ApiError, error) {
   244	        var incr *big.Int
   245	
   246	        // Some header checks must be checked pre proposal.
   247	        if len(hdr) > 0 {
   248	                // Since we encode header len as u16 make sure we do not exceed.
   249	                // Again this works if it goes through but better to be pre-emptive.
   250	                if len(hdr) > math.MaxUint16 {
   251	                        err := fmt.Errorf("JetStream header size exceeds limits for '%s > %s'", jsa.acc().Name, mset.cfg.Name)
   252	                        return hdr, msg, 0, NewJSStreamHeaderExceedsMaximumError(), err
   253	                }
   254	                // Counter increments.
   255	                // Only supported on counter streams, and payload must be empty (if not coming from a source).
   256	                var ok bool
   257	                if incr, ok = getMessageIncr(hdr); !ok {
   258	                        apiErr := NewJSMessageIncrInvalidError()
   259	                        return hdr, msg, 0, apiErr, apiErr
   260	                } else if incr != nil && !sourced {
   261	                        // Only do checks if the message isn't sourced. Otherwise, we need to store verbatim.
   262	                        if !allowMsgCounter {
   263	                                apiErr := NewJSMessageIncrDisabledError()
   264	                                return hdr, msg, 0, apiErr, apiErr
   265	                        } else if len(msg) > 0 {
   266	                                apiErr := NewJSMessageIncrPayloadError()
   267	                                return hdr, msg, 0, apiErr, apiErr
   268	                        } else {
   269	                                // Check for incompatible headers.
   270	                                var doErr bool
   271	                                if getRollup(hdr) != _EMPTY_ ||
   272	                                        getExpectedStream(hdr) != _EMPTY_ ||
   273	                                        getExpectedLastMsgId(hdr) != _EMPTY_ ||
   274	                                        getExpectedLastSeqPerSubjectForSubject(hdr) != _EMPTY_ {
   275	                                        doErr = true
   276	                                } else if _, ok = getExpectedLastSeq(hdr); ok {
   277	                                        doErr = true
   278	                                } else if _, ok = getExpectedLastSeqPerSubject(hdr); ok {
   279	                                        doErr = true
   280	                                }
   281	
   282	                                if doErr {
   283	                                        apiErr := NewJSMessageIncrInvalidError()
   284	                                        return hdr, msg, 0, apiErr, apiErr
   285	                                }
   286	                        }
   287	                }
   288	                // Expected stream name can also be pre-checked.
   289	                if sname := getExpectedStream(hdr); sname != _EMPTY_ && sname != name {
   290	                        return hdr, msg, 0, NewJSStreamNotMatchError(), errStreamMismatch
   291	                }
   292	                // TTL'd messages are rejected entirely if TTLs are not enabled on the stream, or if the TTL is invalid.
   293	                if ttl, err := getMessageTTL(hdr); !sourced && (ttl != 0 || err != nil) {
   294	                        if !allowTTL {
   295	                                return hdr, msg, 0, NewJSMessageTTLDisabledError(), errMsgTTLDisabled
   296	                        } else if err != nil {
   297	                                return hdr, msg, 0, NewJSMessageTTLInvalidError(), err
   298	                        }
   299	                }
   300	                // Check for MsgIds here at the cluster level to avoid excessive CLFS accounting.
   301	                // Will help during restarts.
   302	                if msgId := getMsgId(hdr); msgId != _EMPTY_ {
   303	                        // Dedupe if staged.
   304	                        if _, ok = diff.msgIds[msgId]; ok {
   305	                                return hdr, msg, 0, nil, errMsgIdDuplicate
   306	                        }
   307	                        mset.ddMu.Lock()
   308	                        if dde := mset.checkMsgId(msgId); dde != nil {
   309	                                seq := dde.seq
   310	                                mset.ddMu.Unlock()
   311	                                // Should not return an invalid sequence, in that case error.
   312	                                if seq > 0 {
   313	                                        return hdr, msg, seq, nil, errMsgIdDuplicate
   314	                                } else {
   315	                                        return hdr, msg, 0, NewJSStreamDuplicateMessageConflictError(), errMsgIdDuplicate
   316	                                }
   317	                        }
   318	                        if diff.msgIds == nil {
   319	                                diff.msgIds = map[string]struct{}{msgId: {}}
   320	                        } else {
   321	                                diff.msgIds[msgId] = struct{}{}
   322	                        }
   323	                        mset.ddMu.Unlock()
   324	                }
   325	        }
   326	
   327	        // Apply increment for counter.
   328	        // But only if it's allowed for this stream. This can happen when we store verbatim for a sourced stream.
   329	        if incr == nil && allowMsgCounter {
   330	                apiErr := NewJSMessageIncrMissingError()
   331	                return hdr, msg, 0, apiErr, apiErr
   332	        }
   333	        if incr != nil && allowMsgCounter {
   334	                var initial big.Int
   335	                var sources CounterSources
   336	
   337	                // If we've got a running total, update that, since we have inflight proposals updating the same counter.
   338	                var ok bool
   339	                var counter *msgCounterRunningTotal
   340	                if counter, ok = diff.counter[subject]; ok {
   341	                        initial = *counter.total
   342	                        sources = counter.sources
   343	                } else if counter, ok = mset.clusteredCounterTotal[subject]; ok {
   344	                        initial = *counter.total
   345	                        sources = counter.sources
   346	                        // Make an explicit copy to separate the staged data from what's committed.
   347	                        // Don't need to initialize all values, they'll be overwritten later.
   348	                        counter = &msgCounterRunningTotal{ops: counter.ops}
   349	                } else {
   350	                        // Load last message, and store as inflight running total.
   351	                        var smv StoreMsg
   352	                        sm, err := mset.store.LoadLastMsg(subject, &smv)
   353	                        if err == nil && sm != nil {
   354	                                var val CounterValue
   355	                                // Return an error if the counter is broken somehow.
   356	                                if json.Unmarshal(sm.msg, &val) != nil {
   357	                                        apiErr := NewJSMessageCounterBrokenError()
   358	                                        return hdr, msg, 0, apiErr, apiErr
   359	                                }
   360	                                if ncs := sliceHeader(JSMessageCounterSources, sm.hdr); len(ncs) > 0 {
   361	                                        if err := json.Unmarshal(ncs, &sources); err != nil {
   362	                                                apiErr := NewJSMessageCounterBrokenError()
   363	                                                return hdr, msg, 0, apiErr, apiErr
   364	                                        }
   365	                                }
   366	                                initial.SetString(val.Value, 10)
   367	                        }
   368	                }
   369	                srchdr := sliceHeader(JSStreamSource, hdr)
   370	                if len(srchdr) > 0 {
   371	                        // This is a sourced message, so we can't apply Nats-Incr but
   372	                        // instead should just update the source count header.
   373	                        fields := strings.Split(string(srchdr), " ")
   374	                        origStream := fields[0]
   375	                        origSubj := subject
   376	                        if len(fields) >= 5 {
   377	                                origSubj = fields[4]
   378	                        }
   379	                        var val CounterValue
   380	                        if json.Unmarshal(msg, &val) != nil {
   381	                                apiErr := NewJSMessageCounterBrokenError()
   382	                                return hdr, msg, 0, apiErr, apiErr
   383	                        }
   384	                        var sourced big.Int
   385	                        sourced.SetString(val.Value, 10)
   386	                        if sources == nil {
   387	                                sources = map[string]map[string]string{}
   388	                        }
   389	                        if _, ok = sources[origStream]; !ok {
   390	                                sources[origStream] = map[string]string{}
   391	                        }
   392	                        prevVal := sources[origStream][origSubj]
   393	                        sources[origStream][origSubj] = sourced.String()
   394	                        // We will also replace the Nats-Incr header with the diff
   395	                        // between our last value from this source and this one, so
   396	                        // that the arithmetic is always correct.
   397	                        var previous big.Int
   398	                        previous.SetString(prevVal, 10)
   399	                        incr.Sub(&sourced, &previous)
   400	                        hdr = setHeader(JSMessageIncr, incr.String(), hdr)
   401	                }
   402	                // Now make the change.
   403	                initial.Add(&initial, incr)
   404	                // Generate the new payload.
   405	                var _msg [128]byte
   406	                msg = fmt.Appendf(_msg[:0], "{%q:%q}", "val", initial.String())
   407	                // Write the updated source count headers.
   408	                if len(sources) > 0 {
   409	                        nhdr, err := json.Marshal(sources)
   410	                        if err != nil {
   411	                                return hdr, msg, 0, NewJSMessageCounterBrokenError(), err
   412	                        }
   413	                        hdr = setHeader(JSMessageCounterSources, string(nhdr), hdr)
   414	                }
   415	
   416	                // Check to see if we are over the max msg size.
   417	                maxSize := int64(mset.srv.getOpts().MaxPayload)
   418	                if maxMsgSize >= 0 && int64(maxMsgSize) < maxSize {
   419	                        maxSize = int64(maxMsgSize)
   420	                }
   421	                hdrLen, msgLen := int64(len(hdr)), int64(len(msg))
   422	                // Subtract to prevent against overflows.
   423	                if hdrLen > maxSize || msgLen > maxSize-hdrLen {
   424	                        return hdr, msg, 0, NewJSStreamMessageExceedsMaximumError(), ErrMaxPayload
   425	                }
   426	
   427	                // Keep the in-memory counters up-to-date.
   428	                if counter == nil {
   429	                        counter = &msgCounterRunningTotal{}
   430	                }
   431	                counter.total = &initial
   432	                counter.sources = sources
   433	                counter.ops++
   434	                if diff.counter == nil {
   435	                        diff.counter = map[string]*msgCounterRunningTotal{subject: counter}
   436	                } else {
   437	                        diff.counter[subject] = counter
   438	                }
   439	        }
   440	
   441	        if len(hdr) > 0 {
   442	                // Expected last sequence.
   443	                if seq, exists := getExpectedLastSeq(hdr); exists && seq != mset.clseq-mset.clfs {
   444	                        mlseq := mset.clseq - mset.clfs
   445	                        err := fmt.Errorf("last sequence mismatch: %d vs %d", seq, mlseq)
   446	                        return hdr, msg, 0, NewJSStreamWrongLastSequenceError(mlseq), err
   447	                }
   448	
   449	                // Expected last sequence per subject.
   450	                if seq, exists := getExpectedLastSeqPerSubject(hdr); exists {
   451	                        // Allow override of the subject used for the check.
   452	                        seqSubj := subject
   453	                        if optSubj := getExpectedLastSeqPerSubjectForSubject(hdr); optSubj != _EMPTY_ {
   454	                                seqSubj = optSubj
   455	                        }
   456	
   457	                        // The subject is already written to in this batch, we can't allow
   458	                        // expected checks since they would be incorrect.
   459	                        if _, ok := diff.inflight[seqSubj]; ok {
   460	                                err := errors.New("last sequence by subject mismatch")
   461	                                return hdr, msg, 0, NewJSStreamWrongLastSequenceConstantError(), err
   462	                        }
   463	
   464	                        // If the subject is already in process, block as otherwise we could have
   465	                        // multiple messages inflight with the same subject.
   466	                        if _, found := mset.expectedPerSubjectInProcess[seqSubj]; found {
   467	                                err := errors.New("last sequence by subject mismatch")
   468	                                return hdr, msg, 0, NewJSStreamWrongLastSequenceConstantError(), err
   469	                        }
   470	
   471	                        // If the subject is already in process but without expected headers, block as we would have
   472	                        // multiple messages inflight with the same subject.
   473	                        if _, ok := mset.inflight[seqSubj]; ok {
   474	                                err := errors.New("last sequence by subject mismatch")<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you.     33	func TestJetStreamAtomicBatchPublish(t *testing.T) {
    34	        test := func(
    35	                t *testing.T,
    36	                storage StorageType,
    37	                retention RetentionPolicy,
    38	                replicas int,
    39	        ) {
    40	                c := createJetStreamClusterExplicit(t, "R3S", 3)
    41	                defer c.shutdown()
    42	
    43	                nc, js := jsClientConnect(t, c.randomServer())
    44	                defer nc.Close()
    45	
    46	                var pubAck JSPubAckResponse
    47	
    48	                cfg := &StreamConfig{
    49	                        Name:      "TEST",
    50	                        Subjects:  []string{"foo.*"},
    51	                        Storage:   storage,
    52	                        Retention: retention,
    53	                        Replicas:  replicas,
    54	                }

    56	                _, err := jsStreamCreate(t, nc, cfg)
    57	                require_NoError(t, err)
    58	
    59	                m := nats.NewMsg("foo.0")
    60	                m.Data = []byte("foo.0")
    61	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Id", "uuid")
    62	
    63	                // Publish with atomic publish disabled.
    64	                rmsg, err := nc.RequestMsg(m, time.Second)
    65	                require_NoError(t, err)
    66	                require_NoError(t, json.Unmarshal(rmsg.Data, &pubAck))
    67	                require_NotNil(t, pubAck.Error)
    68	                require_Error(t, pubAck.Error, NewJSAtomicPublishDisabledError())
    69	
    70	                // Enable atomic publish.
    71	                cfg.AllowAtomicPublish = true
    72	                _, err = jsStreamUpdate(t, nc, cfg)
    73	                require_NoError(t, err)
    74	
    75	                // Publish without batch sequence errors.
    76	                rmsg, err = nc.RequestMsg(m, time.Second)
    77	                require_NoError(t, err)
    78	                pubAck = JSPubAckResponse{}
    79	                require_NoError(t, json.Unmarshal(rmsg.Data, &pubAck))
    80	                require_Error(t, pubAck.Error, NewJSAtomicPublishMissingSeqError())
    81	
    82	                // Publish a batch, misses start.
    83	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Id", "uuid")
    84	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Sequence", "2")
    85	                rmsg, err = nc.RequestMsg(m, time.Second)
    86	                require_NoError(t, err)
    87	                pubAck = JSPubAckResponse{}
    88	                require_NoError(t, json.Unmarshal(rmsg.Data, &pubAck))
    89	                require_Error(t, pubAck.Error, NewJSAtomicPublishIncompleteBatchError())
    90	
    91	                // Publish a "batch" which immediately commits.
    92	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Id", "uuid")
    93	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Sequence", "1")
    94	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Commit", "1")
    95	                rmsg, err = nc.RequestMsg(m, time.Second)
    96	                require_NoError(t, err)
    97	                pubAck = JSPubAckResponse{}
    98	                require_NoError(t, json.Unmarshal(rmsg.Data, &pubAck))
    99	                require_Equal(t, pubAck.Sequence, 1)
   100	                require_Equal(t, pubAck.BatchId, "uuid")
   101	                require_Equal(t, pubAck.BatchSize, 1)
   102	
   103	                // Reset commit.
   104	                m.Header.Del("Nats-Batch-Commit")
   105	
   106	                // Publish a "batch" which has gaps.
   107	                require_NoError(t, nc.PublishMsg(m))
   108	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Sequence", "3")
   109	                rmsg, err = nc.RequestMsg(m, time.Second)
   110	                require_NoError(t, err)
   111	                pubAck = JSPubAckResponse{}
   112	                require_NoError(t, json.Unmarshal(rmsg.Data, &pubAck))
   113	                require_Error(t, pubAck.Error, NewJSAtomicPublishIncompleteBatchError())
   114	
   115	                // Publish a batch of N messages.
   116	                m.Header.Del("Nats-Batch-Commit")
   117	                for seq, batch := uint64(1), uint64(5); seq <= batch; seq++ {
   118	                        m.Subject = fmt.Sprintf("foo.%d", seq)
   119	                        m.Data = []byte(m.Subject)
   120	                        m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Sequence", strconv.FormatUint(seq, 10))
   121	                        // If not commit.
   122	                        if seq != batch {
   123	                                require_NoError(t, nc.PublishMsg(m))
   124	                                continue
   125	                        }
   126	
   127	                        m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Commit", "1")
   128	                        rmsg, err = nc.RequestMsg(m, time.Second)
   129	                        require_NoError(t, err)
   130	
   131	                        pubAck = JSPubAckResponse{}
   132	                        require_NoError(t, json.Unmarshal(rmsg.Data, &pubAck))
   133	                        require_Equal(t, pubAck.Sequence, 6)
   134	                        require_Equal(t, pubAck.BatchId, "uuid")
   135	                        require_Equal(t, pubAck.BatchSize, 5)
   136	                }
   137	
   138	                // Validate stream contents.
   139	                if retention != InterestPolicy {
   140	                        for i := 0; i < 6; i++ {
   141	                                rsm, err := js.GetMsg("TEST", uint64(i+1))
   142	                                require_NoError(t, err)
   143	                                subj := fmt.Sprintf("foo.%d", i)
   144	                                require_Equal(t, rsm.Subject, subj)
   145	                                require_Equal(t, string(rsm.Data), subj)
   146	                        }
   147	                }
   148	        }
   149	
   150	        for _, storage := range []StorageType{FileStorage, MemoryStorage} {
   151	                for _, retention := range []RetentionPolicy{LimitsPolicy, InterestPolicy, WorkQueuePolicy} {
   152	                        for _, replicas := range []int{1, 3} {
   153	                                t.Run(fmt.Sprintf("%s/%s/R%d", storage, retention, replicas), func(t *testing.T) {
   154	                                        test(t, storage, retention, replicas)
   155	                                })
   156	                        }
   157	                }
   158	        }
   159	}

   161	func TestJetStreamAtomicBatchPublishLimits(t *testing.T) {
   162	        streamMaxBatchInflightPerStream = 1
   163	        streamMaxBatchInflightTotal = 1
   164	        streamMaxBatchSize = 2
   165	        streamMaxBatchTimeout = 500 * time.Millisecond
   166	        defer func() {
   167	                streamMaxBatchInflightPerStream = streamDefaultMaxBatchInflightPerStream
   168	                streamMaxBatchInflightTotal = streamDefaultMaxBatchInflightTotal
   169	                streamMaxBatchSize = streamDefaultMaxBatchSize
   170	                streamMaxBatchTimeout = streamDefaultMaxBatchTimeout
   171	        }()
   172	
   173	        test := func(t *testing.T, replicas int) {
   174	                c := createJetStreamClusterExplicit(t, "R3S", 3)
   175	                defer c.shutdown()
   176	
   177	                nc := clientConnectToServer(t, c.randomServer())
   178	                defer nc.Close()
   179	
   180	                var pubAck JSPubAckResponse
   181	
   182	                cfg := &StreamConfig{
   183	                        Name:               "FOO",
   184	                        Subjects:           []string{"foo"},
   185	                        Storage:            FileStorage,
   186	                        Retention:          LimitsPolicy,
   187	                        Replicas:           replicas,
   188	                        AllowAtomicPublish: true,
   189	                }
   190	                _, err := jsStreamCreate(t, nc, cfg)
   191	                require_NoError(t, err)
   192	
   193	                // For testing total server-wide maximum inflight batches.
   194	                cfg = &StreamConfig{
   195	                        Name:               "BAR",
   196	                        Subjects:           []string{"bar"},
   197	                        Storage:            FileStorage,
   198	                        Retention:          LimitsPolicy,
   199	                        Replicas:           replicas,
   200	                        AllowAtomicPublish: true,
   201	                }
   202	                _, err = jsStreamCreate(t, nc, cfg)
   203	                require_NoError(t, err)
   204	
   205	                // A batch ID must not exceed the maximum length.
   206	                for _, length := range []int{64, 65} {
   207	                        longBatchId := strings.Repeat("A", length)
   208	                        m := nats.NewMsg("foo")
   209	                        m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Id", longBatchId)
   210	                        m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Sequence", "1")
   211	                        m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Commit", "1")
   212	                        rmsg, err := nc.RequestMsg(m, time.Second)
   213	                        require_NoError(t, err)
   214	                        pubAck = JSPubAckResponse{}
   215	                        require_NoError(t, json.Unmarshal(rmsg.Data, &pubAck))
   216	                        if length <= 64 {
   217	                                require_True(t, pubAck.Error == nil)
   218	                        } else {
   219	                                require_NotNil(t, pubAck.Error)
   220	                                require_Error(t, pubAck.Error, NewJSAtomicPublishInvalidBatchIDError())
   221	                        }
   222	                }
   223	
   224	                // One batch is inflight.
   225	                m := nats.NewMsg("foo")
   226	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Id", "uuid")
   227	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Sequence", "1")
   228	                require_NoError(t, nc.PublishMsg(m))
   229	
   230	                // Another batch moves over the threshold and batch is denied.
   231	                m = nats.NewMsg("foo")
   232	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Id", "exceeds_threshold")
   233	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Sequence", "1")
   234	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Commit", "1")
   235	                rmsg, err := nc.RequestMsg(m, time.Second)
   236	                require_NoError(t, err)
   237	                pubAck = JSPubAckResponse{}
   238	                require_NoError(t, json.Unmarshal(rmsg.Data, &pubAck))
   239	                require_Error(t, pubAck.Error, NewJSAtomicPublishIncompleteBatchError())
   240	
   241	                // Another batch on a different stream moves over the server-wide threshold and batch is denied.
   242	                m = nats.NewMsg("bar")
   243	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Id", "bar")
   244	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Sequence", "1")
   245	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Commit", "1")
   246	                rmsg, err = nc.RequestMsg(m, time.Second)
   247	                require_NoError(t, err)
   248	                pubAck = JSPubAckResponse{}
   249	                require_NoError(t, json.Unmarshal(rmsg.Data, &pubAck))
   250	                require_Error(t, pubAck.Error, NewJSAtomicPublishIncompleteBatchError())
   251	
   252	                // The first batch should now time out.
   253	                sl := c.streamLeader(globalAccountName, "FOO")
   254	                mset, err := sl.globalAccount().lookupStream("FOO")
   255	                require_NoError(t, err)
   256	                checkFor(t, 2*time.Second, 200*time.Millisecond, func() error {
   257	                        mset.mu.RLock()
   258	                        batches := mset.batches
   259	                        mset.mu.RUnlock()
   260	                        if batches == nil {
   261	                                return errors.New("batches not found")
   262	                        }
   263	                        batches.mu.Lock()
   264	                        groups := len(batches.group)
   265	                        batches.mu.Unlock()
   266	                        if groups != 0 {
   267	                                return fmt.Errorf("expected 0 groups, got %d", groups)
   268	                        }
   269	                        return nil
   270	                })
   271	
   272	                // Publishing to the batch should also error since it timed out.
   273	                m = nats.NewMsg("foo")
   274	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Id", "uuid")
   275	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Sequence", "2")
   276	                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Commit", "1")
   277	                rmsg, err = nc.RequestMsg(m, time.Second)
   278	                require_NoError(t, err)
   279	                pubAck = JSPubAckResponse{}
   280	                require_NoError(t, json.Unmarshal(rmsg.Data, &pubAck))
   281	                require_Error(t, pubAck.Error, NewJSAtomicPublishIncompleteBatchError())
   282	
   283	                // Batch should be rejected if going over the max batch size.
   284	                for _, size := range []int{streamMaxBatchSize, streamMaxBatchSize + 1} {
   285	                        for i := range size {
   286	                                seq := i + 1
   287	                                m = nats.NewMsg("foo")
   288	                                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Id", "exceeds_threshold")
   289	                                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Sequence", strconv.Itoa(seq))
   290	                                commit := seq == size
   291	                                if !commit {
   292	                                        require_NoError(t, nc.PublishMsg(m))
   293	                                        continue
   294	                                }
   295	
   296	                                m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Commit", "1")
   297	                                rmsg, err = nc.RequestMsg(m, time.Second)
   298	                                require_NoError(t, err)
   299	                                pubAck = JSPubAckResponse{}
   300	                                require_NoError(t, json.Unmarshal(rmsg.Data, &pubAck))
   301	                                if size <= streamMaxBatchSize {
   302	                                        require_True(t, pubAck.Error == nil)
   303	                                        require_Equal(t, pubAck.BatchSize, size)
   304	                                } else {
   305	                                        require_Error(t, pubAck.Error, NewJSAtomicPublishIncompleteBatchError())
   306	                                }
   307	                        }
   308	                }
   309	        }
   310	
   311	        t.Run("R1", func(t *testing.T) { test(t, 1) })
   312	        t.Run("R3", func(t *testing.T) { test(t, 3) })
   313	}

   373	func TestJetStreamAtomicBatchPublishSourceAndMirror(t *testing.T) {
   374	        test := func(t *testing.T, replicas int) {
   375	                c := createJetStreamClusterExplicit(t, "R3S", 3)
   376	                defer c.shutdown()
   377	
   378	                nc, js := jsClientConnect(t, c.randomServer())
   379	                defer nc.Close()
   380	
   381	                _, err := jsStreamCreate(t, nc, &StreamConfig{
   382	                        Name:               "TEST",
   383	                        Subjects:           []string{"foo"},
   384	                        Storage:            FileStorage,
   385	                        AllowAtomicPublish: true,
   386	                        Replicas:           replicas,
   387	                })
   388	                require_NoError(t, err)
   389	
   390	                for seq := uint64(1); seq <= 3; seq++ {
   391	                        m := nats.NewMsg("foo")
   392	                        m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Id", "uuid")
   393	                        m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Sequence", strconv.FormatUint(seq, 10))
   394	                        commit := seq == 3
   395	                        if !commit {
   396	                                require_NoError(t, nc.PublishMsg(m))
   397	                                continue
   398	                        }
   399	                        m.Header.Set("Nats-Batch-Commit", "1")
   400	
   401	                        rmsg, err := nc.RequestMsg(m, time.Second)
   402	                        require_NoError(t, err)
   403	                        var pubAck JSPubAckResponse
   404	                        require_NoError(t, json.Unmarshal(rmsg.Data, &pubAck))
   405	                        require_Equal(t, pubAck.Sequence, 3)
   406	                        require_Equal(t, pubAck.BatchId, "uuid")
   407	                        require_Equal(t, pubAck.BatchSize, 3)
   408	                }
   409	
   410	                require_NoError(t, js.DeleteMsg("TEST", 2))
   411	                checkFor(t, 2*time.Second, 200*time.Millisecond, func() error {
   412	                        return checkState(t, c, globalAccountName, "TEST")
   413	                })
   414	
   415	                _, err = js.AddStream(&nats.StreamConfig{
   416	                        Name:     "M",
   417	                        Mirror:   &nats.StreamSource{Name: "TEST"},
   418	                        Replicas: replicas,
   419	                })
   420	                require_NoError(t, err)
   421	
   422	                _, err = js.AddStream(&nats.StreamConfig{
   423	                        Name:     "S",
   424	                        Sources:  []*nats.StreamSource{{Name: "TEST"}},
   425	                        Replicas: replicas,
   426	                })
   427	                require_NoError(t, err)
   428	
   429	                checkFor(t, 2*time.Second, 200*time.Millisecond, func() error {
   430	                        for _, name := range []string{"M", "S"} {
   431	                                if si, err := js.StreamInfo(name); err != nil {
   432	                                        return err
   433	                                } else if si.State.Msgs != 2 {
   434	                                        return fmt.Errorf("expected 2 messages for stream %q, got %d", name, si.State.Msgs)
   435	                                }
   436	                        }
   437	                        return nil
   438	                })
   439	
   440	                // Ensure the batching headers were removed when ingested into the source/mirror.
   441	                rsm, err := js.GetMsg("M", 1)
   442	                require_NoError(t, err)
   443	                require_Len(t, len(rsm.Header), 0)
   444	
   445	                rsm, err = js.GetMsg("M", 3)
   446	                require_NoError(t, err)
   447	                require_Len(t, len(rsm.Header), 0)
   448	
   449	                rsm, err = js.GetMsg("S", 1)
   450	                require_NoError(t, err)
   451	                require_Len(t, len(rsm.Header), 1)
   452	                require_Equal(t, rsm.Header.Get(JSStreamSource), "TEST 1 > > foo")
   453	
   454	                rsm, err = js.GetMsg("S", 2)
   455	                require_NoError(t, err)
   456	                require_Len(t, len(rsm.Header), 1)
   457	                require_Equal(t, rsm.Header.Get(JSStreamSource), "TEST 3 > > foo")
   458	        }
   459	
   460	        t.Run("R1", func(t *testing.T) { test(t, 1) })
   461	        t.Run("R3", func(t *testing.T) { test(t, 3) })
   462	}

   464	func TestJetStreamAtomicBatchPublishCleanup(t *testing.T) {
   465	        const (
   466	                Disable = iota
   467	                StepDown
   468	                Delete
   469	                Commit
   470	        )
   471	
   472	        test := func(t *testing.T, mode int) {
   473	                c := createJetStreamClusterExplicit(t, "R3S", 3)

   520	                require_NoError(t, err)
   521	
   522	                mset.mu.RLock()
   523	                batches = mset.batches
   524	                batch = mset.batchApply
   525	                mset.mu.RUnlock()
   526	                require_NotNil(t, batches)
   527	                require_NotNil(t, batch)

   529	                groups := len(batches.grou<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. You should retry this tool after you have searched inside the file with `grep -n` in order to find the line numbers of what you are looking for.</NOTE>

    41	// JetStreamConfig determines this server's configuration.
    42	// MaxMemory and MaxStore are in bytes.
    43	type JetStreamConfig struct {
    44	        MaxMemory    int64         `json:"max_memory"`              // MaxMemory is the maximum size of memory type streams
    45	        MaxStore     int64         `json:"max_storage"`             // MaxStore is the maximum size of file store type streams
    46	        StoreDir     string        `json:"store_dir,omitempty"`     // StoreDir is where storage files are stored
    47	        SyncInterval time.Duration `json:"sync_interval,omitempty"` // SyncInterval is how frequently we sync to disk in the background by calling fsync
    48	        SyncAlways   bool          `json:"sync_always,omitempty"`   // SyncAlways indicates flushes are done after every write
    49	        Domain       string        `json:"domain,omitempty"`        // Domain is the JetStream domain
    50	        CompressOK   bool          `json:"compress_ok,omitempty"`   // CompressOK indicates if compression is supported
    51	        UniqueTag    string        `json:"unique_tag,omitempty"`    // UniqueTag is the unique tag assigned to this instance
    52	        Strict       bool          `json:"strict,omitempty"`        // Strict indicates if strict JSON parsing is performed
    53	}
    54	
    55	// Statistics about JetStream for this server.
    56	type JetStreamStats struct {
    57	        Memory         uint64            `json:"memory"`
    58	        Store          uint64            `json:"storage"`
    59	        ReservedMemory uint64            `json:"reserved_memory"`
    60	        ReservedStore  uint64            `json:"reserved_storage"`
    61	        Accounts       int               `json:"accounts"`
    62	        HAAssets       int               `json:"ha_assets"`
    63	        API            JetStreamAPIStats `json:"api"`
    64	}
    65	
    66	type JetStreamAccountLimits struct {
    67	        MaxMemory            int64 `json:"max_memory"`
    68	        MaxStore             int64 `json:"max_storage"`
    69	        MaxStreams           int   `json:"max_streams"`
    70	        MaxConsumers         int   `json:"max_consumers"`
    71	        MaxAckPending        int   `json:"max_ack_pending"`
    72	        MemoryMaxStreamBytes int64 `json:"memory_max_stream_bytes"`
    73	        StoreMaxStreamBytes  int64 `json:"storage_max_stream_bytes"`
    74	        MaxBytesRequired     bool  `json:"max_bytes_required"`
    75	}

    79	        Store          uint64                 `json:"storage"`
    80	        ReservedMemory uint64                 `json:"reserved_memory"`
    81	        ReservedStore  uint64                 `json:"reserved_storage"`

    84	        Limits         JetStreamAccountLimits `json:"limits"`

  6096	        maxMsgSize, lseq := int(mset.cfg.MaxMsgSize), mset.lseq
  6097	        isLeader, isClustered, isSealed, allowRollup, denyPurge, allowTTL, allowMsgCounter, allowMsgSchedules, allowAtomicPublish := mset.isLeader(), mset.isClustered(), mset.cfg.Sealed, mset.cfg.AllowRollup, mset.cfg.DenyPurge, mset.cfg.AllowMsgTTL, mset.cfg.AllowMsgCounter, mset.cfg.AllowMsgSchedules, mset.cfg.AllowAtomicPublish
  6098	        mset.mu.RUnlock()
  6099	
  6100	        // If message tracing (with message delivery), we will need to send the
  6101	        // event on exit in case there was an error (if message was not proposed).
  6102	        // Otherwise, the event will be sent from processJetStreamMsg when
  6103	        // invoked by the leader (from applyStreamEntries).
  6104	        if mt != nil {
  6105	                defer func() {
  6106	                        if retErr != nil {
  6107	                                mt.sendEventFromJetStream(retErr)
  6108	                        }
  6109	                }()
  6110	        }
  6111	
  6112	        // Check that we are the leader. This can be false if we have scaled up from an R1 that had inbound queued messages.
  6113	        if !isLeader {
  6114	                return NewJSClusterNotLeaderError()
  6115	        }
  6116	
  6117	        // Bail here if sealed.
  6118	        if isSealed {
  6119	                var resp = JSPubAckResponse{PubAck: &PubAck{Stream: mset.name()}, Error: NewJSStreamSealedError()}
  6120	                b, _ := json.Marshal(resp)
  6121	                mset.outq.sendMsg(reply, b)
  6122	                return NewJSStreamSealedError()
  6123	        }
  6124	
  6125	        // Check here pre-emptively if we have exceeded this server limits.
  6126	        if js.limitsExceeded(stype) {
  6127	                s.resourcesExceededError(stype)
  6128	                if canRespond {
  6129	                        b, _ := json.Marshal(&JSPubAckResponse{PubAck: &PubAck{Stream: name}, Error: NewJSInsufficientResourcesError()})
  6130	                        outq.send(newJSPubMsg(reply, _EMPTY_, _EMPTY_, nil, b, nil, 0))
  6131	                }
  6132	                // Stepdown regardless.
  6133	                if node := mset.raftNode(); node != nil {
  6134	                        node.StepDown()
  6135	                }
  6136	                return NewJSInsufficientResourcesError()
  6137	        }
  6138	
  6139	        // Check here pre-emptively if we have exceeded our account limits.
  6140	        if exceeded, err := jsa.wouldExceedLimits(st, tierName, r, subject, hdr, msg); exceeded {
  6141	                if err == nil {
  6142	                        err = NewJSAccountResourcesExceededError()
  6143	                }
  6144	                s.RateLimitWarnf("JetStream account limits exceeded for '%s': %s", jsa.acc().GetName(), err.Error())
  6145	                if canRespond {
  6146	                        var resp = &JSPubAckResponse{PubAck: &PubAck{Stream: name}}
  6147	                        resp.Error = err
  6148	                        response, _ = json.Marshal(resp)
  6149	                        outq.send(newJSPubMsg(reply, _EMPTY_, _EMPTY_, nil, response, nil, 0))
  6150	                }
  6151	                return err
  6152	        }
  6153	
  6154	        // Check msgSize if we have a limit set there. Again this works if it goes through but better to be pre-emptive.
  6155	        // Subtract to prevent against overflows.
  6156	        if maxMsgSize >= 0 && (len(hdr) > maxMsgSize || len(msg) > maxMsgSize-len(hdr)) {
  6157	                err := fmt.Errorf("JetStream message size exceeds limits for '%s > %s'", jsa.acc().Name, mset.cfg.Name)
  6158	                s.RateLimitWarnf("%s", err.Error())
  6159	                if canRespond {
  6160	                        var resp = &JSPubAckResponse{PubAck: &PubAck{Stream: name}}
  6161	                        resp.Error = NewJSStreamMessageExceedsMaximumError()
  6162	                        response, _ = json.Marshal(resp)
  6163	                        outq.send(newJSPubMsg(reply, _EMPTY_, _EMPTY_, nil, response, nil, 0))
  6164	                }
  6165	                return err
  6166	        }
  6167	
  6168	        if !allowAtomicPublish {
  6169	                err := NewJSAtomicPublishDisabledError()
  6170	                if canRespond {
  6171	                        b, _ := json.Marshal(&JSPubAckResponse{PubAck: &PubAck{Stream: name}, Error: err})
  6172	                        outq.send(newJSPubMsg(reply, _EMPTY_, _EMPTY_, nil, b, nil, 0))
  6173	                }
  6174	                return err
  6175	        }
  6176	
  6177	        // Batch ID is too long.
  6178	        if len(batchId) > 64 {
  6179	                err := NewJSAtomicPublishInvalidBatchIDError()
  6180	                if canRespond {
  6181	                        b, _ := json.Marshal(&JSPubAckResponse{PubAck: &PubAck{Stream: name}, Error: err})
  6182	                        outq.send(newJSPubMsg(reply, _EMPTY_, _EMPTY_, nil, b, nil, 0))
  6183	                }
  6184	                return err
  6185	        }
  6186	
  6187	        batchSeq, exists := getBatchSequence(hdr)
  6188	        if !exists {
  6189	                err := NewJSAtomicPublishMissingSeqError()
  6190	                if canRespond {
  6191	                        b, _ := json.Marshal(&JSPubAckResponse{PubAck: &PubAck{Stream: name}, Error: err})
  6192	                        outq.send(newJSPubMsg(reply, _EMPTY_, _EMPTY_, nil, b, nil, 0))
  6193	                }
  6194	                return err
  6195	        }
  6196	        commit := len(sliceHeader(JSBatchCommit, hdr)) != 0
  6197	
  6198	        mset.mu.Lock()
  6199	        if mset.batches == nil {
  6200	                mset.batches = &batching{
  6201	                        group: make(map[string]*batchGroup, 1),
  6202	                }
  6203	        }
  6204	        batches := mset.batches
  6205	        mset.mu.Unlock()
  6206	
  6207	        respondIncompleteBatch := func() error {
  6208	                err := NewJSAtomicPublishIncompleteBatchError()
  6209	                if canRespond {
  6210	                        buf, _ := json.Marshal(&JSPubAckResponse{PubAck: &PubAck{Stream: name}, Error: err})
  6211	                        outq.send(newJSPubMsg(reply, _EMPTY_, _EMPTY_, nil, buf, nil, 0))
  6212	                }
  6213	                return err
  6214	        }
  6215	
  6216	        // Get batch.
  6217	        batches.mu.Lock()
  6218	        b, ok := batches.group[batchId]
  6219	        if !ok {
  6220	                if batchSeq != 1 {
  6221	                        batches.mu.Unlock()
  6222	                        return respondIncompleteBatch()
  6223	                }
  6224	
  6225	                // Limits.
  6226	                maxInflightPerStream := streamMaxBatchInflightPerStream
  6227	                maxInflightTotal := streamMaxBatchInflightTotal
  6228	                opts := s.getOpts()
  6229	                if opts.JetStreamLimits.MaxBatchInflightPerStream > 0 {
  6230	                        maxInflightPerStream = opts.JetStreamLimits.MaxBatchInflightPerStream
  6231	                }
  6232	                if opts.JetStreamLimits.MaxBatchInflightTotal > 0 {
  6233	                        maxInflightTotal = opts.JetStreamLimits.MaxBatchInflightTotal
  6234	                }
  6235	
  6236	                // Confirm we can facilitate an additional batch.
  6237	                if len(batches.group)+1 > maxInflightPerStream {
  6238	                        batches.mu.Unlock()
  6239	                        return respondIncompleteBatch()
  6240	                }
  6241	
  6242	                // Confirm we'll not exceed the server limit.
  6243	                if globalInflightBatches.Add(1) > int32(maxInflightTotal) {
  6244	                        globalInflightBatches.Add(-1)
  6245	                        batches.mu.Unlock()
  6246	                        return respondIncompleteBatch()
  6247	                }
  6248	
  6249	                var err error
  6250	                if b, err = batches.newBatchGroup(mset, batchId); err != nil {
  6251	                        globalInflightBatches.Add(-1)
  6252	                        batches.mu.Unlock()
  6253	                        return respondIncompleteBatch()
  6254	                }
  6255	                batches.group[batchId] = b
  6256	        }
  6257	
  6258	        // Detect gaps.
  6259	        b.lseq++
  6260	        if b.lseq != batchSeq {
  6261	                b.cleanupLocked(batchId, batches)
  6262	                batches.mu.Unlock()
  6263	                return respondIncompleteBatch()
  6264	        }
  6265	
  6266	        // Confirm the batch doesn't exceed the allowed size.
  6267	        maxSize := streamMaxBatchSize
  6268	        if maxBatchSize := s.getOpts().JetStreamLimits.MaxBatchSize; maxBatchSize > 0 {
  6269	                maxSize = maxBatchSize
  6270	        }
  6271	        if batchSeq > uint64(maxSize) {
  6272	                b.cleanupLocked(batchId, batches)
  6273	                batches.mu.Unlock()
  6274	                return respondIncompleteBatch()
  6275	        }
  6276	
  6277	        // Persist, but optimize if we're committing because we already know last.
  6278	        // If the underlying store is file-based we need to persist everything to survive hard kills, because we're R1.
  6279	        if !commit || b.store.Type() == FileStorage {
  6280	                seq, _, err := b.store.StoreMsg(subject, hdr, msg, 0)
  6281	                if err != nil || seq != batchSeq {
  6282	                        b.cleanupLocked(batchId, batches)
  6283	                        batches.mu.Unlock()
  6284	                        return respondIncompleteBatch()
  6285	                }
  6286	        }
  6287	        if !commit {
  6288	                batches.mu.Unlock()
  6289	                return nil
  6290	        }
  6291	
  6292	        // Ensure the batch is prepared for the commit and will not be cleaned up while committing.
  6293	        if !b.readyForCommit() {
  6294	                // Don't do cleanup, this is already done.
  6295	                batches.mu.Unlock()
  6296	                return respondIncompleteBatch()
  6297	        }
  6298	
  6299	        // Proceed with proposing the batch.
  6300	        ts := time.Now().UnixNano()
  6301	
  6302	        // Need to hold this lock even if we're not clustered, because we'll
  6303	        // be accessing state that requires this lock (even if it's empty).
  6304	        mset.clMu.Lock()
  6305	
  6306	        // We only use mset.clseq for clustering and in case we run ahead of actual commits.
  6307	        // Check if we need to set initial value here
  6308	        if isClustered && (mset.clseq == 0 || mset.clseq < lseq+mset.clfs) {
  6309	                // Need to unlock and re-acquire the locks in the proper order.
  6310	                mset.clMu.Unlock()
  6311	                // Locking order is stream -> batchMu -> clMu
  6312	                mset.mu.RLock()
  6313	                batch := mset.batchApply
  6314	                var batchCount uint64
  6315	                if batch != nil {
  6316	                        batch.mu.Lock()
  6317	                        batchCount = batch.count
  6318	                }
  6319	                mset.clMu.Lock()
  6320	                // Re-capture
  6321	                lseq = mset.lseq
  6322	                mset.clseq = lseq + mset.clfs + batchCount
  6323	                // Keep hold of the mset.clMu, but unlock the others.
  6324	                if batch != nil {
  6325	                        batch.mu.Unlock()
  6326	                }
  6327	                mset.mu.RUnlock()
  6328	        }
  6329	
  6330	        rollback := func(seq uint64) {
  6331	                if isClustered {
  6332	                        // TODO(mvv): reset in-memory expected header maps
  6333	                        mset.clseq -= seq - 1
  6334	                }
  6335	                mset.clMu.Unlock()
  6336	        }
  6337	
  6338	        errorOnUnsupported := func(seq uint64, header string) *ApiError {
  6339	                apiErr := NewJSAtomicPublishUnsupportedHeaderBatchError(header)
  6340	                rollback(seq)
  6341	                b.cleanupLocked(batchId, batches)
  6342	                batches.mu.Unlock()
  6343	                if canRespond {
  6344	                        buf, _ := json.Marshal(&JSPubAckResponse{PubAck: &PubAck{Stream: name}, Error: apiErr})
  6345	                        outq.send(newJSPubMsg(reply, _EMPTY_, _EMPTY_, nil, buf, nil, 0))
  6346	                }
  6347	                return apiErr
  6348	        }
  6349	
  6350	        var (
  6351	                entries []*Entry
  6352	                bsubj   string
  6353	                bhdr    []byte
  6354	                bmsg    []byte
  6355	                apiErr  *ApiError
  6356	                err     error
  6357	                smv     StoreMsg
  6358	                sm      *StoreMsg
  6359	                sz      int
  6360	        )
  6361	
  6362	        diff := &batchStagedDiff{}
  6363	        for seq := uint64(1); seq <= batchSeq; seq++ {
  6364	                if seq == batchSeq && b.store.Type() != FileStorage {
  6365	                        bsubj, bhdr, bmsg = subject, hdr, msg
  6366	                } else if sm, err = b.store.LoadMsg(seq, &smv); sm != nil && err == nil {
  6367	                        bsubj, bhdr, bmsg = sm.subj, sm.hdr, sm.msg
  6368	                } else {
  6369	                        rollback(seq)
  6370	                        b.cleanupLocked(batchId, batches)
  6371	                        batches.mu.Unlock()
  6372	                        return respondIncompleteBatch()
  6373	                }
  6374	
  6375	                // Reject unsupported headers.
  6376	                if msgId := getMsgId(bhdr); msgId != _EMPTY_ {
  6377	                        return errorOnUnsupported(seq, JSMsgId)
  6378	                }
  6379	                if getExpectedLastMsgId(hdr) != _EMPTY_ {
  6380	                        return errorOnUnsupported(seq, JSExpectedLastMsgId)
  6381	                }
  6382	
  6383	                if bhdr, bmsg, _, apiErr, err = checkMsgHeadersPreClusteredProposal(diff, mset, subject, bhdr, bmsg, false, name, jsa, allowRollup, denyPurge, allowTTL, allowMsgCounter, allowMsgSchedules, discard, discardNewPer, maxMsgSize, maxMsgs, maxMsgsPer, maxBytes); err != nil {
  6384	                        rollback(seq)
  6385	                        b.cleanupLocked(batchId, batches)
  6386	                        batches.mu.Unlock()
  6387	                        if canRespond {
  6388	                                buf, _ := json.Marshal(&JSPubAckResponse{PubAck: &PubAck{Stream: name}, Error: apiErr})
  6389	                                outq.send(newJSPubMsg(reply, _EMPTY_, _EMPTY_, nil, buf, nil, 0))
  6390	                        }
  6391	                        return err
  6392	                }
  6393	
  6394	                if isClustered {
  6395	                        var _reply string
  6396	                        isCommit := seq == batchSeq
  6397	                        if isCommit {
  6398	                                _reply = reply
  6399	                        }
  6400	                        esm := encodeStreamMsgAllowCompressAndBatch(bsubj, _reply, bhdr, bmsg, mset.clseq, ts, false, batchId, seq, isCommit)
  6401	                        entries = append(entries, newEntry(EntryNormal, esm))
  6402	                        mset.clseq++
  6403	                        sz += len(esm)
  6404	                }
  6405	        }
  6406	
  6407	        // Commit batch.
  6408	        if !isClustered {
  6409	                for seq := uint64(1); seq <= batchSeq; seq++ {
  6410	                        if seq == batchSeq && b.store.Type() != FileStorage {
  6411	                                bsubj, bhdr, bmsg = subject, hdr, msg
  6412	                        } else if sm, err = b.store.LoadMsg(seq, &smv); sm != nil && err == nil {
  6413	                                bsubj, bhdr, bmsg = sm.subj, sm.hdr, sm.msg
  6414	                        } else {
  6415	                                // Should not happen, we've already checked this message existed while doing consistency checks.
  6416	                                // We'll just exit here, the batch is already inconsistent without the message at this sequence.
  6417	                                // No use in trying to still store the rest.
  6418	                                break
  6419	                        }
  6420	                        var _reply string
  6421	                        if seq == batchSeq {
  6422	                                _reply = reply
  6423	                        }
  6424	                        mset.processJetStreamMsg(bsubj, _reply, bhdr, bmsg, 0, 0, mt, false)
  6425	                }
  6426	        } else {
  6427	                // Do a single multi proposal. This ensures we get to push all entries to the proposal queue in-order
  6428	                // and not interleaved with other proposals.
  6429	                diff.commit(mset)
  6430	                if err := node.ProposeMulti(entries); err == nil {
  6431	                        mset.trackReplicationTraffic(node, sz, r)
  6432	                } else {
  6433	                        // TODO(mvv): reset in-memory expected header maps
  6434	                        mset.clseq -= batchSeq
  6435	                }
  6436	
  6437	                // Check to see if we are being overrun.
  6438	                // TODO(dlc) - Make this a limit where we drop messages to protect ourselves, but allow to be configured.
  6439	                if mset.clseq-(lseq+mset.clfs) > streamLagWarnThreshold {
  6440	                        lerr := fmt.Errorf("JetStream stream '%s > %s' has high message lag", jsa.acc().Name, name)
  6441	                        s.RateLimitWarnf("%s", lerr.Error())
  6442	                }
  6443	        }
  6444	        mset.clMu.Unlock()
  6445	        b.cleanupLocked(batchId, batches)
  6446	        batches.mu.Unlock()
  6447	        return nil
  6448	}
  6449	
  6450	// Used to signal inbound message to registered consumers.
  6451	type cMsg struct {
  6452	        seq  uint64
  6453	        subj string
  6454	}
  6455	
  6456	// Pool to recycle consumer bound msgs.
  6457	var cMsgPool sync.Pool
  6458	
  6459	// Used to queue up consumer bound msgs for signaling.
  6460	func newCMsg(subj string, seq uint64) *cMsg {
  6461	        var m *cMsg
  6462	        cm := cMsgPool.Get()
  6463	        if cm != nil {
  6464	                m = cm.(*cMsg)
  6465	        } else {
  6466	                m = new(cMsg)
  6467	        }
  6468	        m.subj, m.seq = subj, seq
  6469	
  6470	        return m
  6471	}
  6472	
  6473	func (m *cMsg) returnToPool() {
  6474	        if m == nil {
  6475	                return
  6476	        }
  6477	        m.subj, m.seq = _EMPTY_, 0
  6478	        cMsgPool.Put(m)
  6479	}
  6480	
  6481	// Go routine to signal consumers.
  6482	// Offloaded from stream msg processing.
  6483	func (mset *stream) signalConsumersLoop() {
  6484	        mset.mu.RLock()
  6485	        s, qch, sch, msgs := mset.srv, mset.qch, mset.sch, mset.sigq
  6486	        mset.mu.RUnlock()
  6487	
  6488	        for {
  6489	                select {
  6490	                case <-s.quitCh:
  6491	                        return
  6492	                case <-qch:
  6493	                        return
  6494	                case <-sch:
  6495	                        cms := msgs.pop()
  6496	                        for _, m := range cms {
  6497	                                seq, subj := m.seq, m.subj
  6498	                                m.returnToPool()
  6499	                                // Signal all appropriate consumers.
  6500	                                mset.signalConsumers(subj, seq)

  3518	func (js *jetStream) applyStreamMsgOp(mset *stream, op entryOp, mbuf []byte, isRecovering bool) error {
  3519	        s := js.srv
  3520	
  3521	        if op == compressedStreamMsgOp {
  3522	                var err error
  3523	                mbuf, err = s2.Decode(nil, mbuf)
  3524	                if err != nil {
  3525	                        panic(err.Error())
  3526	                }
  3527	        }
  3528	
  3529	        subject, reply, hdr, msg, lseq, ts, sourced, err := decodeStreamMsg(mbuf)
  3530	        if err != nil {
  3531	                if node := mset.raftNode(); node != nil {
  3532	                        s.Errorf("JetStream cluster could not decode stream msg for '%s > %s' [%s]",
  3533	                                mset.account(), mset.name(), node.Group())
  3534	                }
  3535	                panic(err.Error())
  3536	        }
  3537	
  3538	        // Check for flowcontrol here.
  3539	        if len(msg) == 0 && len(hdr) > 0 && reply != _EMPTY_ && isControlHdr(hdr) {
  3540	                if !isRecovering {
  3541	                        mset.sendFlowControlReply(reply)
  3542	                }
  3543	                return nil
  3544	        }
  3545	
  3546	        // Grab last sequence and CLFS.
  3547	        last, clfs := mset.lastSeqAndCLFS()
  3548	
  3549	        // We can skip if we know this is less than what we already have.
  3550	        if lseq-clfs < last {
  3551	                s.Debugf("Apply stream entries for '%s > %s' skipping message with sequence %d with last of %d",
  3552	                        mset.account(), mset.name(), lseq+1-clfs, last)
  3553	                mset.mu.Lock()
  3554	                // Check for any preAcks in case we are interest based.
  3555	                mset.clearAllPreAcks(lseq + 1 - clfs)
  3556	                mset.mu.Unlock()
  3557	                return nil
  3558	        }
  3559	
  3560	        // Skip by hand here since first msg special case.
  3561	        // Reason is sequence is unsigned and for lseq being 0
  3562	        // the lseq under stream would have to be -1.
  3563	        if lseq == 0 && last != 0 {
  3564	                return nil
  3565	        }
  3566	
  3567	        // Messages to be skipped have no subject or timestamp or msg or hdr.
  3568	        if subject == _EMPTY_ && ts == 0 && len(msg) == 0 && len(hdr) == 0 {
  3569	                // Skip and update our lseq.
  3570	                last := mset.store.SkipMsg()
  3571	                mset.mu.Lock()
  3572	                mset.setLastSeq(last)
  3573	                mset.clearAllPreAcks(last)
  3574	                mset.mu.Unlock()
  3575	                return nil
  3576	        }
  3577	
  3578	        var mt *msgTrace
  3579	        // If not recovering, see if we find a message trace object for this
  3580	        // sequence. Only the leader that has proposed this entry will have
  3581	        // stored the trace info.
  3582	        if !isRecovering {
  3583	                mt = mset.getAndDeleteMsgTrace(lseq)
  3584	        }
  3585	        // Process the actual message here.
  3586	        err = mset.processJetStreamMsg(subject, reply, hdr, msg, lseq, ts, mt, sourced)
  3587	
  3588	        // If we have inflight make sure to clear after processing.
  3589	        // TODO(dlc) - technically check on inflight != nil could cause datarace.
  3590	        // But do not want to acquire lock since tracking this will be rare.
  3591	        if mset.inflight != nil {
  3592	                mset.clMu.Lock()
  3593	                if i, found := mset.inflight[subject]; found {
  3594	                        // Decrement from pending operations. Once it reaches zero, it can be deleted.
  3595	                        if i.ops > 0 {
  3596	                                var sz uint64
  3597	                                if mset.store.Type() == FileStorage {
  3598	                                        sz = fileStoreMsgSizeRaw(len(subject), len(hdr), len(msg))
  3599	                                } else {
  3600	                                        sz = memStoreMsgSizeRaw(len(subject), len(hdr), len(msg))
  3601	                                }
  3602	                                if i.bytes >= sz {
  3603	                                        i.bytes -= sz
  3604	                                } else {
  3605	                                        i.bytes = 0
  3606	                                }
  3607	                                i.ops--
  3608	                        }
  3609	                        if i.ops == 0 {
  3610	                                delete(mset.inflight, subject)
  3611	                        }
  3612	                }
  3613	                mset.clMu.Unlock()
  3614	        }
  3615	
  3616	        // Update running total for counter.
  3617	        if mset.clusteredCounterTotal != nil {
  3618	                mset.clMu.Lock()
  3619	                if counter, found := mset.clusteredCounterTotal[subject]; found {
  3620	                        // Decrement from pending operations. Once it reaches zero, it can be deleted.
  3621	                        if counter.ops > 0 {
  3622	                                counter.ops--
  3623	                        }
  3624	                        if counter.ops == 0 {
  3625	                                delete(mset.clusteredCounterTotal, subject)
  3626	                        }
  3627	                }
  3628	                mset.clMu.Unlock()
  3629	        }
  3630	
  3631	        // Clear expected per subject state after processing.
  3632	        if mset.expectedPerSubjectSequence != nil {
  3633	                mset.clMu.Lock()
  3634	                if subj, found := mset.expectedPerSubjectSequence[lseq]; found {
  3635	                        delete(mset.expectedPerSubjectSequence, lseq)
  3636	                        delete(mset.expectedPerSubjectInProcess, subj)
  3637	                }
  3638	                mset.clMu.Unlock()
  3639	        }
  3640	
  3641	        if err != nil {
  3642	                if err == errLastSeqMismatch {
  3643	
  3644	                        var state StreamState
  3645	                        mset.store.FastState(&state)
  3646	
  3647	                        // If we have no msgs and the other side is delivering us a sequence past where we
  3648	                        // should be reset. This is possible if the other side has a stale snapshot and no longer
  3649	                        // has those messages. So compact and retry to reset.
  3650	                        if state.Msgs == 0 {
  3651	                                mset.store.Compact(lseq + 1)
  3652	                                // Retry
  3653	                                err = mset.processJetStreamMsg(subject, reply, hdr, msg, lseq, ts, mt, sourced)
  3654	                        }
  3655	                        // FIXME(dlc) - We could just run a catchup with a request defining the span between what we expected
  3656	                        // and what we got.
  3657	                }
  3658	
  3659	                // Only return in place if we are going to reset our stream or we are out of space, or we are closed.
  3660	                if isClusterResetErr(err) || isOutOfSpaceErr(err) || err == errStreamClosed {
  3661	                        return err
  3662	                }
  3663	                s.Debugf("Apply stream entries for '%s > %s' got error processing message: %v",
  3664	                        mset.account(), mset.name(), err)
  3665	        }
  3666	        return nil
  3667	}
  3668	
  3669	// Returns the PeerInfo for all replicas of a raft node. This is different than node.Peers()
  3670	// and is used for external facing advisories.
  3671	func (s *Server) replicas(node RaftNode) []*PeerInfo {
  3672	        var replicas []*PeerInfo
  3673	        for _, rp := range node.Peers() {
  3674	                if sir, ok := s.nodeToInfo.Load(rp.ID); ok && sir != nil {
  3675	                        si := sir.(nodeInfo)
  3676	                        pi := &PeerInfo{Peer: rp.ID, Name: si.name, Current: rp.Current, Offline: si.offline, Lag: rp.Lag}
  3677	                        if !rp.Last.IsZero() {
  3678	                                pi.Active = time.Since(rp.Last)
  3679	                        }
  3680	                        replicas = append(replicas, pi)
  3681	                }
  3682	        }
  3683	        return replicas
  3684	}
